 The Delhi High Court on Thursday granted relief to Greenpeace activist Priya Pillai and canceled the look out notice issued against her
 priya ko janvari 2015 main landan ke liye udaan bharne vaale vimaan se neeche utaar diya gaya tha

 Pillai was invited to London to discuss his campaign among local communities in the great region of Madhya Pradesh

 ) Rajpal Singh, who captained the Indian hockey team that won medals at the Commonwealth and Asian Games, accused the country's hockey management of not working in the national interest and said that the plight of hockey will continue till the team has stability and lakhs
 Despite efforts, we cannot do well internationally
 hockey punjab kii ore se yojit punjab ekadash or bharat ke bich pradarshnee match khilne pahunche purv bhartiya captain ne baatcheet main kaha, ‘‘desh main hockey ke liye kuch bhi acha nahin ho rahaa he
 Hockey management is not doing any work in the national interest and its negative impact is being seen on the game
 ’’ Rajpal, who is captaining the Punjab XI, said, "if everything goes on like this and efforts continue to serve personal interests, then the plight of hockey in India will also continue
" ham lakh koshish kar len, apni puraani form main nahin aa sakate kyonki yahaan khel ko kaise unnat kiya jaae, ise chhodkar har kaam ho rahaa he
 '' yah poochne par ki aap iske liye kise jimmedaar maanate hai, rashtramandal khelon main rajat padak jeetne vaale raajapaal ne kaha, ‘‘main kisi vyakti vishesh kii baat nahin kar rahaa hum
 i am talking about the entire hockey management, who are ignoring the interest of the country or the interest of hockey
 iskaa asar khel par ho rahaa he
 '' asian khelon main kaansya padak vijeta team kii captaini kar chuke raajapaal ne kaha, ‘‘team main sthirataa kaa abhaav he
 The better-performing player does not see a place in the team
 iskaa asar unke pradarshan par padataa he
 a player who performs better in one tournament is not selected in the team for the next tournament
 ’’ He also said, "I was the captain, the team got a bronze medal in the Asian Games
" maine captain ke pad se istipha de diya
 After this, when the team went to play Sultan Azlan Shah tournament, i was not selected
 aise kai khilaadi hai jo behatar pradarshan karte hai or unhen nahin chunaa jaataa isliye yah jaruri he ki team main sthirataa ho
 '' raajapaal ne kaha, ‘‘vishwa series hockey main achche achche khilaadi khel rahe hai lekin hockey prabandhan yaa team ke chayankarta un khilaadiyon ko ‘raajnneeti’ kii vajah se rashtriya team nahin chunate, is ‘raajnneeti’ kaa asar khel par hota he
 The result is our embarrassing performance in the Olympics
 ’’ He also considers the captains to be replaced again for the decline in hockey
 raajapaal kaa kahana he, ‘‘na to captain ko pataa hota he or na hi khilaadiyon ko ki agle toornament main ve chune jaaenge yaa nahin
 This affects their performance
 pichley chah saal main aap najar daalenge to pataa chalegaa ki saat se adhik baar captain badale ja chuke hai
 '' Comments jab yah poocha gaya ki maaikel nobs or unke pehle ke coach ke saath aap kaam kar chuke hai, donon main se kis coach kaa pradarshan badhiya he to raajapaal ne hansate hue kaha, ‘‘main is bare main kuch nahin kahuunga
 Yes, it is surprising that the coach who made the team to win a medal at the Commonwealth Games was terminated and his tenure in the Olympics was extended
 ’’ The former captain said that no matter where the coach brought the hockey management, the game will not be good in the country until it is removed from personal interests

 It is published directly from the Syndicate feed
 ) Rangpanchami is celebrated on Krishna Panchami of Chaitra month, just five days after Holi
 is baar rangapanchami 6 march ko manaai jaaegi
 This festival is especially celebrated in Maharashtra, Gujarat and Madhya Pradesh
 desh ke kuch anya hisson main bhi log ise dhoomdhaam se manaate hai
 Rangpanchami is a part of Holi
 holi kaa utsav caitra maas kii krishna pratipada se lekar panchami tak chalata he
 Even on Krishna Panchami, people watch with gulal
 isliye ise rang panchami kaha jaataa he
 Rang Panchami is a special festival in the Konkan region
 log maanate hai ki hawa main rang udaane par or ek-duusare ko lagane par vibhinn rangon kii ore devtaa aakarshith hote hai
 This makes the atmosphere a combination of positive waves in the universe and the sensation of the respective gods in the color particles
 mana jaataa he ki is din vaataavaran main udate hue gulaal vyakti main sakaaratmak gunon bharte hai or nakaaratmakataa kaa naash karte hai
 What is the northeast angle in Vastu, which Modi mentioned in his speech? According to beliefs, a person has rajas and tam qualities which produce negative energy
 is din log puure shahar main rangarang juluus nikaalte hai
 a special type of sweet dish is also made in homes on Rang Panchami
 jise puuranpoli kaha jaataa he
 Chaitra month is fruitful, so do worship and worship is a celebration of the glory of the universe
 vividh tejotsav tarangon ke bhraman se brahmad main anek rang aavashyaktaa ke anusaar saakaar hote hai tathaa sambandhit ghatak ke kaary ke liye poorak va poshak vaataavaran kii nirmit karte hai
 On this day, elements of different deities are attracted towards the color particles of different colors being blown into the atmosphere
 brahmad main karyrat sakaaratmak tarangon ke sanyog se hokar jeev ko devtaa ke sparsh kii anubhuti dekar devtaa aashirvad dete hai
 a 37-year-old police constable was killed by a suspect in a robbery case in Ahmedabad, Gujarat, inside the office of the city's high-security crime branch
 aparaadh ko anjaam dene ke baad vah ghatnasthal se faraar ho gaya
 Post mortem of the body is being done
 aparaadh shakha main teen-stareey suraksha ke baavjood aparaadhon ko sulajhane main ati khyaati praapt vishisht bal kii chhavi ko is ghatana se dhakka laga he
 After about three hours, the body of the constable was recovered from the interrogation room in the morning
 police inspector aar aar sirvaiya ke mutabik, ek history-shiter or maadak padaarthon ke vyapaar main shaamil manish balai ne consteble chandrakant makvaana kihatyaki he
 Makwana was questioning Balai between 2 pm and 4 am
 sandigdh ne police consteble ke sir or chehre par lohe ke chad se hamalaa kiya
 The murder took place in the wee hours of Thursday, where Balai was kept in custody
 hampostmortmke baad maut ke nishchit kaaran ke bare main jaan sakenge
 The body was found three hours after the murder
 bijepi saansad shatrughna sinha ne kaha ki agar unki party ne unhen bihar main mukhyamantri daavedaar ke rup main pesh kiya hota to shaayad chunaav ke nattejey kuch or hote
 Shatrughan told India TV, "I am not boasting
 lekin main mahasoos karata hum ki jab bihari logon kaa laadla, dhartiputra, vaastavik bihari babu ko jaan boojhkar kinare laga diya gaya to iskaa nishchit hi mere samarthakon or prashansakon par bura prabhaav padaa
 " unhone kaha, "main nahin kah saktaa ki isse kitna fark padataa, lekin itnaa nishchit rup se kah saktaa hum
 
 
 We would definitely get more seats than we have got
 " sinha ne is bare main kuch nahin kaha ki kya purv up mukhyamantri susheel modi ne chunaav prachaar main unhen kinare lagaaya
 He said, "we all belong to the same family and we have to learn from defeat while introspecting and accountability instead of anything else
 jaise ki aarake singh, jo ki purv grih sachiv hai or ek paripakv vyakti hai, ne kaha ki aatmamanthan hona chahie, javabdehi tay honi chahie
 With this, we will take defeat as a challenge and turn it into an opportunity for ourselves
 " Targeting the BJP leadership to put leaders from outside the state in election management, Shatrughan said, "A large number of leaders were called from outside
 koi punjab se tha, koi maharashtra se to koi dilli se
 All these were completely cut off from the ground reality
 inhen na to yahaan ke jatigat samikarnon kii samaj thi or na hi sthaneey boliyon kii
 " unhone kaha, "is tarah ke log yahaan ek saath maheenon ek saath rahe
 So much money, talent and energy was spent
 or, nateeja kya niklaa? hamane dilli kii haar se kuch nahin siikhaa
 This shows frustration
 ham buree tarah haare or isse mujhe dukh hua
 " shatrughna ne kaha, "main pehle bhi kah chukaa hum or phir doharaa rahaa hum- bijepi meri pehali or sambhavat: aakhri party he
 i came to the party when it had only two mps
 aaj iske paas bahumat he
 "comments sinha ne pradhanmantri narendra modi kii bihar main itani adhik reliyon par sawaal uthaate hue kaha ki ham kyon nahin pradhanmantri kaa boj kam karte? kya hamen nahin aage laayaa janaa chahie tha? He said that he is always available if the party considers his utility
 unhone kaha, "main apni party ke saath hum
 
 apane joshilay pradhanmantri narendra modi kaa haath majboot karne ke liye
 " shatrughna ne india tivi se kaha, "main shekhi nahin baghaar rahaa hum
 But i feel that when the Bihari people were killed off the ladla, the earth, the real Bihari Babu, it definitely had a bad effect on my supporters and fans
 " He said, "I can't say how much it makes a difference, but i can say so definitely
 
 
 hamen jitani seat mili hai, nishchit rup se usase adhik milteen
 "sinha did not say anything about whether former Deputy Chief Minister Sushil Modi sidelined him in the election campaign
 unhone kaha, "ham sabhi ek hi parivaar ke hai or hamen kuch or kii bajaay aatmamanthan karte hue haar se siikhnaa hoga or javabdehi tay kerani hogi
 For example, RK Singh, a former home secretary and a mature man, said that there should be introspection, accountability should be fixed
 isse ham haar ko chunauti kii tarah lenge or ise apane liye ek avasar main badal denge
 " bijepi netritv par rajya ke baahar ke netaaon ko chunaav prabandhan main lagane par nishaanaa sadhate hue shatrughna ne kaha, "badi sankhya main netaa baahar se bulaae gaye
 Some were from Punjab, some from Maharashtra and some from Delhi
 ye sabhi jamini hakeekat se bilkul kate hue the
 He neither had an understanding of the caste equations here nor the local dialects
 " He said, "people like this stayed here for months together
 itnaa paisa, pratibha or urja kharch hui

 yah hataasha ko dikhaata he
 We lost badly and it hurt me
 " Shatrughan said, "I have said this before and then i am repeating - BJP is my first and probably last party

 " ingine main kharabi aane ke kaaran 70 yatriyon ko lekar coimbatore se hyderabad ja rahe spice jet ke ek vimaan ko bengalooru main utaara gaya
 Airline sources said the pilots of the Bombardier Q-400, flying Flight SG 1048, received signs of an engine malfunction on the cockpit panel, following which it was decided to land the aircraft at the Bengaluru airport
 hawaii adde ke adhikariyon ne bataaya ki fire brigade or ambulance samet sabhi apaat sevaaon ko taiyaar rakhaa gaya tha, taaki vimaan surakshit rup se land kar sake
 After landing, the passengers were sent to Hyderabad by another flight
 punjab ke moga main chalati bas main chhedchhad ke baad dhakele jane ke kaaran jaan ganvaane vaali kishori ke pita ne punjab sarkaar kii muaavje or rojgaar kii peshkash sweekaar kar lee or mritka ke shav kaa postmortem tathaa uskaa antim sanskaar karne par raji ho gaye
 After this, the four-day-long protest over the incident ended and the teenager was cremated
 kishori ke shav kaa ravivaar raat kareeb aath baj kar 35 minute par uske gaanv landeke main kadi suraksha ke bich antim sanskaar kar diya gaya
 The prayer was given by his father, who said that there was no agreement with the state government to remove the deadlock
 buudhvaar ko moga main hue is haadase ko lekar sharmindagi or aalochana kaa saamana kar rahe mukhyamantri prakaash singh badal ne mritak ke pita or parivaar ke anya sadasyon se shaam ko mulaakaat kii or unke saath kareeb 30 minute bitaye
 Badal described the incident as 'unbearable' and 'painful', while the police said that the four accused have been arrested
 mritak ke pita ne samvaadadaataaon ko bataaya 'main yah aagrah karnaa chahta hum ki main apni beti kaa antim sanskaar karnaa chahta hum
 He also said that he agreed to conduct the post-mortem without any pressure
 kishori ke pita purv main uskaa antim sanskaar karne se yah kehete hue manaa kar rahe the ki jab tak up mukhyamantri sukhbir singh badal or orbit aviation ke anya logon ke khilaaf maamla darj nahin kiya jaataa, tab tak vah apni beti kaa antim sanskaar nahin karenge
 The victim's father also demanded the cancellation of the license for the Orbit Aviation bus service
 sukhbir is bas company ke maalikon main se ek hai
 The teenager's father sat on a dharna with some local politicians to assert his demand
 unhone kaha 'rajya sarkaar ne hamen jo peshkash kii he vah mujhe sweekaar he
 He (the state government) fulfilled our demands and assured that the killers of my daughter would be punished
 ' Regarding the compensation, he said that he is not aware of the amount
 'main nahin kah saktaa ki kitni kshatipurti he
 Whatever is given to me is enough for me
 mujhe khushi he ki main apni beti ke saath yahaan se jaaunga
 ' purv main sarkaar ne 20 lakh rupaye kii kshatipurti or ghayal maa ke liye naukari, uskaa muft ilaaj kiye jone kii peshkash kii thi or yah bhi kaha tha ki maamle kii sunwaayee fast trek adaalat main hogi
 But the victim's family declined the offer
 tippaniyan Moga Deputy Commissioner Parminder Singh Gill said that instead of the district administration, Orbit Aviation, the owner of the bus, will give a compensation of Rs 24 lakh to the victim's family
